&amp;= \boldsymbol{0}, \\ \boldsymbol{r}_2 &amp;= 0.5\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}}, \\ \boldsymbol{r}_t &amp;= 0.2\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\[1.5ex] \boldsymbol{r}_{t1} &amp;= 0.2\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ r_{t1} &amp;= 0.2\ m, \\ \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t1}} &amp;= \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\[1.5ex] \boldsymbol{r}_{t2} &amp;= -0.5\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + 0.2\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ r_{t2} &amp;= \frac{\sqrt{29}}{10}\ m, \\ \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t2}} &amp;= -\frac{5 \sqrt{29}}{29}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + \frac{2 \sqrt{29}}{29}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\[1.5ex] \boldsymbol{E}_1 &amp;= k_e \frac{Q_1}{r_{t1}^2} \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t1}} \\ &amp;= 2250\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ \boldsymbol{E}_2 &amp;= k_e \frac{Q_2}{r_{t2}^2} \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t2}} \\ &amp;= -\frac{18000}{29}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t2}} \\ &amp;= \frac{90000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} - \frac{36000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ &amp;\approx 576.3\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} - 230.52\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ \boldsymbol{E} &amp;= \boldsymbol{E}_1 + \boldsymbol{E}_2 \\ &amp;= \frac{90000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + \left(2250 - \frac{36000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\right)\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ &amp;\approx 576.3\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + 2019.48\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ E &amp;\approx 2100.1\ NC^{-1}. \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*}  \lambda &amp;= \frac{dq}{dl} \implies dq = \lambda\ dl = \lambda\ dy, \\  r &amp;= \sqrt{y^2 + s^2}, \\  dE &amp;= k_e \frac{dq}{r^2} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \frac{dy}{y^2 + s^2}, \\  d E_x &amp;= \cos \alpha_1\ dE, \\  d E_y &amp;= \sin \alpha_1\ dE, \\  \cos \alpha_1 &amp;= \frac{s}{r}, \\  \sin \alpha_1 &amp;= -\sin \alpha_2 = -\frac{y}{r}, \\  d E_x &amp;= k_e \lambda s \frac{dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}}, \\  E_x &amp;= k_e \lambda s \int_{-h_y}^{l - h_y} \frac{dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}} \\  &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \left[\frac{y}{\sqrt{y^2 + s^2}}\right]_{-h_y}^{l - h_y} \\  &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \left[\frac{l - h_y}{\sqrt{(l - h_y)^2 + s^2}} + \frac{h_y}{\sqrt{h_y^2 + s^2}}\right], \\  d E_y &amp;= k_e \lambda \frac{y\ dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}}, \\  E_y &amp;= -k_e \lambda \int_{-h_y}^{l - h_y} \frac{y\ dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \left[\frac{1}{\sqrt{y^2 + s^2}}\right]_{-h_y}^{l - h_y} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \left[\frac{1}{\sqrt{y^2 + s^2}}\right]_{-h_y}^{l - h_y} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \left[\frac{1}{\sqrt{(l - h_y)^2 + s^2}} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{h_y^2 + s^2}}\right]. \\ \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*}  E_x &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \lim_{l \to \infty} \left(\frac{l - \frac{l}{2}}{\sqrt{\left(l - \frac{l}{2}\right)^2 + s^2}} + \frac{\frac{l}{2}}{\sqrt{\left(\frac{l}{2}\right)^2 + s^2}}\right) \\  &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \lim_{l \to \infty} \left(\frac{\frac{l}{2}}{\sqrt{\left(\frac{l}{2}\right)^2 + s^2}} + \frac{\frac{l}{2}}{\sqrt{\left(\frac{l}{2}\right)^2 + s^2}}\right) \\  &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \lim_{l \to \infty} \left(\frac{l}{\sqrt{\frac{l^2 + 4s^2}{4}}}\right) \\  &amp;= \frac{2 k_e \lambda}{s} \lim_{l \to \infty} \left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{1 + 4\frac{s^2}{l^2}}}\right) \\  &amp;= \frac{2 k_e \lambda}{s}.
